That does include a compiler, assembler, linker and other programs required to build and debug Zephyr applications.\n- Only the SDK files of the targeted MCU may be installed\n- **Zephyr RTOS Version Support:**\n  - Samples are Validated<sup>1</sup> with **Zephyr RTOS v4.2 & Zephyr SDK v0.17.0.**\n  - Samples are Buildable<sup>1</sup> with **Zephyr RTOS v3.7.0 LTS & Zephyr SDK v0.16.9.** (see [Supported Boards & Shields](#supported-boards--shields) for limitations)\n- Follow steps [here](https://docs.zephyrproject.org/4.2.0/develop/getting_started/index.html#install-the-zephyr-sdk) to install/update the Zephyr SDK on your specific platform. This needs to be done only once.\n- Ensure your SDK is compliant with the used version of Zephyr RTOS : https://github.com/zephyrproject-rtos/sdk-ng/wiki/Zephyr-Version-Compatibility\n- To use other Setup\n\n<details>\n<summary><b>Standalone Workspace (Simplest for Evaluation)</b></summary>\n<br>\n\nInstall USP Zephyr in a different directory than your default upstream zephyr installation:\n\n```bash\n# Create and initialize workspace\nmkdir zephyr_workspace\ncd zephyr_workspace\ngit clone https://github.com/Lora-net/usp_zephyr.git\nwest init -l usp_zephyr\nwest update\n```\n\nYou can check that the module is correctly recognized by Zephyr:\n\n```bash\nwest list usp_zephyr\n```\n\nNotes:\n- USP Zephyr is used as the manifest repository.\n- The Zephyr installation & USP Zephyr Setup was tested for both Linux & Windows Development OS.\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n<summary><b>Integration in Custom application</b></summary>\n<br>\n\nExample of https://xxxxx application\n```\n\nEdit there your `application/west.yml` manifest file choosing the revision of ups_zephyr & ups :\n<div style=\"display: flex; gap: 2em;\">\n  <div>\n    <h3>Simple dependency description</h3>\n    <pre>\nmanifest:\n  projects:\n    - name: usp_zephyr\n      path: usp_zephyr\n      url: https://github.com/Lora-net/usp_zephyr.git\n      revision: develop\n      import: true\n  self:\n    path: application\n    </pre>\n  </div>\n  <div>\n    <h3>Advanced dependency description with selected versions</h3>\n    <pre>\nmanifest:\n  projects:\n    - name: https://github.com/Lora-net/usp_zephyr.git\n      revision: v1.0.0\n    - name: usp\n      path: modules/lib/usp\n      url: https://github.com/Lora-net/usp.git\n      revision: v1.0.0\n      submodules: true\n  self:\n    path: application\n    </pre>\n  </div>\n</div>\n\nand do :\n```bash\nwest init -l application\nwest update\n```\n\nWork in your source files in `application_zephyr_workspace/application`\n```bash\napplication/my_project\n├── boards\n├── CMakeLists.txt\n├── prj.conf\n├── README.rst\n└── src\n```\n\nAnd compile & flash as usual :\n```bash\nwest build --board xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_wio_lr2021 application/xxx\nwest flash\n```\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n<summary><b>Integration in NCS workspace (experimental)</b></summary>\n<br>\n\n**WARNING : This integration is experimental as the official validated integration is for Zephyr RTOS v4.2**\n\nCan be used for T2/T3 topology.\nEdit `nrf/west.yml` (or your manifest):\n\n   ```yaml\n   manifest:\n     projects:\n       - name: usp_zephyr\n         path: modules/usp_zephyr\n         url: https://github.com/Lora-net/usp_zephyr.git\n         revision: feature/usp_zephyr\n         import: true\n   ```\n\nUpdate workspace:\n   ```bash\n   west update\n   ```\n\nCheck that the module is correctly detected by Zephyr:\n\n```bash\nwest list usp_zephyr\n```\n\nInstall **pyOCD**:\n   ```bash\n   pip install pyocd\n   ```\n\n**WARNING DISABLE SYSBUILD**\n- At compilation, use the `--no-sysbuild` parameter :\n```\nwest build --pristine --board <board> --shield <shield> --no-sysbuild\n```\n\n</details>\n\n\n## Build and Run in the Standalone Workspace\n\nUsing the Semtech LoRa Plus Xiao EVK (Xiao-nRF54L15 + LR2021-Wio) on `periodical_uplink` sample :\n\n```bash\ncd zephyr_workspace\nwest build --pristine --board xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_wio_lr2021 usp_zephyr/samples/usp/lbm/periodical_uplink\nwest flash\n```\n\nAll samples are located in [`samples/usp`](samples/usp/README.md) directory, you can use any supported board/shield as define in next section to build and flash other samples semtech_wio_lr2021` |\n\n    > <sup>1</sup> `Validated` : passed the Semtech nominal validation process.<br>`Buildable` : can be compiled but did not go through full Semtech validation process and can be considered experimental.<br>`Might work` : was compiled and tested on `periodical_uplink` sample only with low validation\n    >\n    > **<sup>2</sup> XIAO ESP32 Binary Blobs**\n    > Espressif HAL requires RF binary blobs in order work. Run the command below to retrieve those files before west build.\n    > ```\n    > west blobs fetch hal_espressif\n    > ```\n    > **<sup>3</sup> WIO-LR2021 CN version** ⚠️\n    > For WIO-LR2021 China (CN) versions the PA table configuration `tx-power-cfg-lf`defined in `usp_zephyr/boards/shields/semtech_wio_lr20xx/semtech_wio_lr20xx_common.dtsi` need to be adjusted as defined in LR2021 Datasheet page 134 to (CN - 490Mhz) band for optimal performances. Look for the 2 `470MHz` prefilled tables in the `semtech_wio_lr20xx_common.dtsi` file.\n\n-   **Flashing**\n\n    The Xiao-nRF54 doesn't embeds a J-Link interface, it is instead interfaced with a CMSIS-DAP interface.\n    We recommend using `pyocd`, version >= 0.38.0 for both flashing and debugging. By default, `pyocd` should be included when installing Zephyr requirements, it will be intalled inside the venv. Use `pyocd --version` to check the installed version. Use `pip install pyocd` if it is not already installed.\n    On Debian-based systems, you may need to install additional udev rules to be able to connect to the board. You might want to follow the instructions [here](https://github.com/pyocd/pyOCD/tree/main/udev) to install PyOCD known USB devices. Additionaly, you will have to manually install `99-xiao-nrf54l15.rules` file found in `usp_zephyr/boards/seeed/xiao_nrf54l15/support` using the same procedure.\n\n    In case you want to flash with native pyocd command, you can run:\n    ```bash\n    pyocd flash -t nrf54l ./build_xiao/zephyr/zephyr.hex # Replace build_xiao with your build folder name\n    ```\n    If you encounter an error saying the the board is locked, run\n    ```bash\n    pyocd erase -c --target nrf54l\n    ```\n    <br>\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n<summary><strong>STMicro [NUCLEO-L476RG] and [NUCLEO-U575ZI-Q]</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\n-   **Supported Zephyr:** Validated<sup>1</sup> on 4.2 (buildable<sup>1</sup> on v3.7.0 LTS)\n\n-   **MCU board build option**\n\n    >   | Type | Status<sup>1</sup> | Image | Command |\n    >   |------|--------|--------|---------|\n    >   | [**Nucleo-L476RG**](https://www.st.com/en/evaluation-tools/nucleo-l476rg.html) | Validated | <img src=\"doc/assets/Nucleo_L476RG.png\" width=\"60\"/> | `--board nucleo_l476rg/stm32l476xx` |\n    >   | [**Nucleo-U575ZI-Q**](https://www.st.com/en/evaluation-tools/nucleo-u575zi-q.html)| Buildable |<img src=\"doc/assets/Nucleo_U575ZI_Q.png\" width=\"60\"/> | `--board nucleo_u575zi_q/stm32u575xx` |\n\n-   **RF shield build option**\n\n    >   | Type | Status<sup>1</sup> | Image | Command |\n    >   |------|--------|--------|---------|\n    >   | **Wio-LR2021 LoRa Plus Expansion Board<sup>3</sup>** | Validated for Nucleo-L476RG | <img src=\"doc/assets/LoRa_Plus_Expansion_Board_wio.png\" width=\"80\"/> | <code>--shield semtech_mbed_wio_interface --shield semtech_wio_lr2021</code> or <code>--shield semtech_mbed_wio_interface --shield semtech_loraplus_expansion_board  --shield semtech_wio_lr2021</code> |\n    >   | **LR11xx (multi-option)** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/LR1110.jpg\" width=\"80\"/> | `--shield semtech_lr1110mb1xxs` or <br> `--shield semtech_lr1120mb1xxs` or<br>`--shield semtech_lr1121mb1xxs` |\n    >   | **SX126x** | Buildabled | <img src=\"doc/assets/SX1261.jpg\" width=\"80\"/> | e.g. `--shield semtech_sx1261mb2bas` (cf. [boards/shields/semtech_sx126xmb2xxs](boards/shields/semtech_sx126xmb2xxs)) |\n\n    > <sup>1</sup> `Validated` : passed the Semtech nominal validation process.<br>`Buildable` : can be compiled but did not go through full Semtech validation process and can be considered experimental.<br>`Might work` : was compiled and tested on `periodical_uplink` sample only with low validation\n    >\n    > **<sup>3</sup> WIO-LR2021 CN version** ⚠️\n    > For WIO-LR2021 China (CN) versions the PA table configuration `tx-power-cfg-lf`defined in `usp_zephyr/boards/shields/semtech_wio_lr20xx/semtech_wio_lr20xx_common.dtsi` need to be adjusted as defined in LR2021 Datasheet page 134 to (CN - 490Mhz) band for optimal performances. Look for the 2 `470MHz` prefilled tables in the `semtech_wio_lr20xx_common.dtsi` file.\n\n-   **Flashing**\n\n    STM32 chips use ST-Link as interface, and are programmed using STM32CubeProgrammer tool. You might want to [download and install STM32CubeProg](https://www.st.com/en/development-tools/stm32cubeprog.html) from ST website. Then, Zephyr should be able to locate the installation folder and use the tool.\n\n<br>\n\n</details>\n\n\n<details>\n<summary><strong>Nordic [nRF54L15 DK] and [nRF52840 DK]</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\n-   **Supported Zephyr:**\n    -   nRF52840 DK: Buildable<sup>3</sup> on 4.2 & v3.7.0 LTS)\n    -   nRF54l15 DK: Buildable<sup>3</sup> on 4.2\n\n\n-   **MCU board build option**\n\n    >   | Type | Status<sup>1</sup> | Image | Command |\n    >   |------|--------|--------|---------|\n    >   | [**nRF52840 DK**](https://www.nordicsemi.com/Products/Development-hardware/nRF52840-DK) | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/nRF52840_DK.png\" width=\"60\"/> | `--board nrf52840dk/nrf52840` |\n    >   | [**nRF54l15 DK**](https://www.nordicsemi.com/Products/Development-hardware/nRF54L15-DK) | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/nRF54L15_DK.png\" width=\"60\"/> | `--board nrf54l15dk/nrf54l15/cpuapp` |\n\n\n-   **RF shield build option for nRF54l15 DK**\n\n    >   | Type | Status<sup>1</sup> | Image | Command[<sup>2</sup> |\n    >   |------|--------|--------|---------|\n    >   | **Wio-LR2021<br>LoRa Plus Expansion Board<sup>3</sup>** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/LoRa_Plus_Expansion_Board_wio.png\" width=\"80\"/> | `--shield semtech_nrf54l15dk_mbed_interface --shield semtech_mbed_wio_interface --shield semtech_wio_lr2021` |\n    >   | **LR11xx<br>(multi-option)** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/LR1110.jpg\" width=\"80\"/>   | <code>--shield semtech_nrf54l15dk_mbed_interface --shield semtech_lr1110mb1xxs</code> or <code>--shield semtech_nrf54l15dk_mbed_interface --shield semtech_lr1120mb1xxs</code> or <code>--shield semtech_nrf54l15dk_mbed_interface --shield semtech_lr1121mb1xxs</code> |\n    >   | **SX126x** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/SX1261.jpg\" width=\"80\"/> | e.g. <code>--shield semtech_nrf54l15dk_mbed_interface --shield semtech_sx1261mb2bas</code> (cf. [boards/shields/semtech_sx126xmb2xxs](boards/shields/semtech_sx126xmb2xxs)) |\n    <br>\n\n-   **RF shield build option for nRF52840 DK**\n\n    >   | Type | Status<sup>1</sup> | Image | Command<sup>2</sup> |\n    >   |------|--------|--------|---------|\n    >   | **Wio-LR2021<br>LoRa Plus Expansion Board<sup>3</sup>** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/LoRa_Plus_Expansion_Board_wio.png\" width=\"80\"/> | `--shield semtech_mbed_wio_interface --shield semtech_wio_lr2021` |\n    >   | **LR11xx<br>(multi-option)** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/LR1110.jpg\" width=\"80\"/>   | `--shield semtech_lr1110mb1xxs`<br>`--shield semtech_lr1120mb1xxs`<br>`--shield semtech_lr1121mb1xxs` |\n    >   | **SX126x** | Buildable | <img src=\"doc/assets/SX1261.jpg\" width=\"80\"/> | e.g. `--shield semtech_sx1261mb2bas` (cf. [boards/shields/semtech_sx126xmb2xxs](boards/shields/semtech_sx126xmb2xxs)) |\n    <br>\n\n    > <sup>1</sup> `Validated` : passed the Semtech nominal validation process.<br>`Buildable` : can be compiled but did not go through full Semtech validation process and can be considered experimental.<br>`Might work` : was compiled and tested on `periodical_uplink` sample only with low validation\n    >\n    > **<sup>2</sup> nRF54L15 DK interface** ⚠️\n    > The **nRF54L15-DK** does not provide an Arduino-compatible header like the other Nordic DK boards. Because of this, a separate interface/adapter board is required to connect Semtech shields.\n    > The **--shield semtech_mbed_wio_interface** option must be added so that the correct pin mapping is applied when building the project.\n    > The mandatory pins are:\n    >> | nRF54L15-DK Pin | Arduino connector Pin | LRXXxx shield pin function |\n    >> | --------------- | --------------------- | -------------------------- |\n    >> | P0.00 | A0 | LR_NRESET |\n    >> | P1.06 | D7 | NSS |\n    >> | P1.11 | D3 | BUSY |\n    >> | P1.12 | D5 | DIO9 |\n    >> | P2.06 | D13 | SPI_SCK |\n    >> | P2.08 | D11 | SPI_MOSI |\n    >> | P2.09 | D12 | SPI_MISO |\n    >>\n    > The mandatory pin for geoloc example on shield embedding a LNA is:\n    >> | nRF54L15-DK Pin | Arduino connector Pin | LRXXxx shield pin function |\n    >> | --------------- | --------------------- | -------------------------- |\n    >> | P1.13 | A3 | LNA_CTRL_MCU |\n    >\n    > Other pins:\n    >> | nRF54L15-DK Pin | Arduino connector Pin | LRXXxx shield pin function |\n    >> | --------------- | --------------------- | -------------------------- |\n    >> | P0.01 | A5 | LED_RX |\n    >> | P0.02 | A4 | LED_TX |\n    >> | P0.03 | D14 | I2C_SDA |\n    >> | P0.04 | D15 | I2C_SCL |\n    > **<sup>3</sup> WIO-LR2021 CN version** ⚠️\n    > For WIO-LR2021 China (CN) versions the PA table configuration `tx-power-cfg-lf`defined in `usp_zephyr/boards/shields/semtech_wio_lr20xx/semtech_wio_lr20xx_common.dtsi` need to be adjusted as defined in LR2021 Datasheet page 134 to (CN - 490Mhz) band for optimal performances. Look for the 2 `470MHz` prefilled tables in the `semtech_wio_lr20xx_common.dtsi` file.\n\n-   **Flashing**\n    For Nordic DKs, you will need:\n    - the Nordic `nrfutil` tool (alongside with its `device` module) installed and available in your PATH. Also, please note that `nrfjprog` tool by Nordic is deprecated and doesn't include support for latest Nordic CPUs such as nRF54 series, so it is recommended to always use `nrfutil`.\n    Please visit [here](https://docs.nordicsemi.com/bundle/nrfutil/page/guides/installing.html) for a guide on how to install `nrfutil` and its `device` module.\n    - SEGGER J-Link drivers, available on [Segger website](https://www.segger.com/downloads/jlink/). Download and install the driver corresponding to your system.\n    <br>\n</details>\n<br>\n\nThanks to the Zephyr ecosystem, the USP module can be ported to almost any MCU platform, enabling deployment across [850+ supported hardware](https://docs.zephyrproject.org/latest/boards/index.html#) targets, please follow the [USP porting guide](doc/usp_zephyr_porting_guide.md) for more information.\n\n## Guides & Advanced Topics\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>USP architecture</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\nFor an in-depth explanation of system components, interactions, and design principles, refer to [USP Architecture](doc/USP_Architecture.md).\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>Samples Documentation</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\nFor more details on Samples, refs to [`samples/usp`](samples/usp/README.md).\n\n</details>\n\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>USP Integration in VS Code</strong></summary>\n    <br>\n\nFiles provided to support VS Code integration are :\n- `usp_zephyr_workspace.code-workspace`\n- Build & flash : `.vscode/tasks.json` (to be update to local user host configuration)\n- Debug : `.vscode/launch.json` (to be update to local user host configuration)\n\nOpen the VS Code Workspace file (File->Open Workspace from file) : `usp_zephyr/usp_zephyr_workspace.code-workspace` to load USP integration in VS Code.\n\nThe configuration is for both Windows & Linux.\nPython virtual environment location and zephyr sdk path can be set in [settings.json](.vscode/settings.json)\n\n**CTRL-SHIFT-P** will allow you to run tasks :\n- West Build\n- West Interactive Build\n- West Flash\n\n**F5** will allow you to run & debug.\n\nDefault configuration is for\n- Radios\n- LoRa Plus dev kit + xiao nRF54l15,\n- Wio LR2021,\n- with Cortex-Debug extension from marus25.\n\nFor other MCU and radio boards, modify tasks.json & launch.json.\n\n### Debugging the samples (`launch.json`)\n\nThis section presents how to debug the sample from within VSCode environment using `Cortex-Debug` extension. As the name implies, this extension is designed for debugging Cortex-based MCUs.\n\nWe will use as example the nRF52840-DK Development Kit board embedding the nRF52840 MCU.\n\nThis section shows the configuration for debugging with zephyr SDK GDB tool using\n- Xiao nRF54 with pyOCD\n- STM32L476RG with openocd\n- nRF52840 DK with JLink\n- nRF54l15 DK with JLink\n\nThe installation steps of openocd, jlink is not covered by this documentation. Please refer to those tools installation guide.\n\nEdit the [`launch.json`](.vscode/launch.json) configuration file:\n- Change the `gdbPath` in [settings.json](.vscode/settings.json) to point to zephyr SDK debugger. `arm-zephyr-eaby-gdb` executable is typically located in the Zephyr SDK folder.\n- You may have to update `executable` if you changed the location of build directory. Typically, zephyr.elf is generated in a `build/zephyr` folder.\n- You can comment/uncomment `preLaunchTask` field if you want to automatically build your project before debugging it.\n\n### Build in VS Code\n\nThe first solution is to open a Terminal and use the compilation command lines described above.\n\nAlternately, you may tune the provided `tasks.json` file to\n- your west environment\n- your MCU & radio boards\n- your application : path & compilation flags\n\nBelow is an excerpt from the tasks.json file for the \"West Build\" task :\n```json\n{\n\t\"version\": \"2.0.0\",\n\t\"tasks\": [\n        {\n            \"label\": \"West Build\",\n            \"type\": \"shell\",\n            \"group\": {\n                \"kind\": \"build\",\n                \"isDefault\": true\n            },\n            \"options\": {\n                \"cwd\": \"${workspaceFolder:Zephyr Workspace}\",\n            },\n            \"linux\": {\n \"${workspaceFolder:Zephyr Workspace}\\\\..\\\\zephyrproject\\\\.venv\\\\Scripts\\\\west.exe\",\n                \"args\": [\n                    \"build\",\n                    \"--pristine\",\n                    \"auto\",\n                    \"--board\",\n                    \"xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp\",\n                    \"--shield\",\n                    \"semtech_wio_lr2021\",\n                    \"${workspaceFolder:LoRa MultiProtocol SW Platform for Zephyr}\\\\samples\\\\usp\\\\sdk\\\\ranging_demo\",\n                    \"--\",\n                    \"-DCMAKE_EXPORT_COMPILE_COMMANDS=ON\", \"-DEXTRA_CFLAGS=\\\"-DRANGING_DEVICE_MODE=RANGING_DEVICE_MODE_SUBORDINATE\\\"\",\n                ],\n            },\n            \"osx\": {\n                \"command\": \"${workspaceFolder:Zephyr Workspace}/../zephyrproject/.venv/bin/west\",\n                \"args\": [\n                    \"build\",\n                    \"--pristine\",\n                    \"auto\",\n                    \"--board\",\n                    \"xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp\",\n                    \"--shield\",\n                    \"semtech_wio_lr2021\",\n \"-DEXTRA_CFLAGS=\\\"-DRANGING_DEVICE_MODE=RANGING_DEVICE_MODE_SUBORDINATE\\\"\",\n                ],\n            },\n            \"problemMatcher\": []\n        },\n\n```\n\nThe user has to update\n- the installation path of west in [settings.json](.vscode/settings.json)\n- `${workspaceFolder:LoRa MultiProtocol SW Platform for Zephyr}/samples/usp/sdk/ranging_demo`with the application path ,\n- `-DEXTRA_CFLAGS=\\\"-DRANGING_DEVICE_MODE=RANGING_DEVICE_MODE_SUBORDINATE\\\"` with the compilation flags\n\nThe user may want to update\n- the default MCU board `xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp`\n- the default radio board `semtech_wio_lr2021`\n\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>Logging & Debugging</strong></summary>\n    <br>\n\n-   **Output Messages**\n\n    The samples uses Zephyr's `logging` api to oputput logging messages. Then, depending on the board, these messages are sent to the user, typically via a UART link. On all boards officialy supported by Semtech, the logs are sent simply via UART to a debugger IC present on the board, that exposes (at least) one CDC interface (Virtual Serial/COM Port) on its USB interface. Some boards may expose more than one port to the host computer, and only one will be used.\n    Any serial terminal software can be used to read data. On Unix systems, `gtkterm` is recommended as it handles ANSI color formatting used by LBM in its output messages. On Windows, `TeraTerm` can be used. \\\n    Default config is **115200 baud, 8 data bits, 1 stop bit, no parity, no flow control**. \\\n    The ANSI color formatting can be disabled in the sample prj.conf via the `CONFIG_LOG_BACKEND_SHOW_COLOR` Kconfig option.\n\n-   **Debugging**\n\n    **LoRa Plus© EVK**\n\n    The nRF54L15\n    - supports up to 4 hardware breakpoints.\n    - uses the Serial Wire Debug (SWD) interface for debugging and programming.\n\n    The XIAO nRF54L15\n    - contains a SAMD11 with CMSIS-DAP interface, allowing flashing (even drag'n'drop), debugging, logging, over the USB port.\n    - is compatible with usual debugging tools, such as J-Link from SEGGER, OpenOCD, pyOCD.\n\n    The LoRa Plus© EVK\n    - exposes a SWD Programming Interface (through pogo pins underneasth the XIAO nRF54L15) for usual debugging & advanced debugging like RTT / SWO, update of CMSIS-DAP,\n    - allow to use compatible advanced SWD debugging probes.\n    - depending on your EVK, the XIAO wiring to the SWD connector may not be available.\n\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>Porting USP to a new MCU board or RF shield</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\nThis [chapter](doc/usp_zephyr_porting_guide.md) explains how to port USP Zephyr module\n- on other MCU\n- on other RF radio PCB (Shield)\n\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n<summary><strong>Porting Legacy LoRa Basics Modem (LBM) to USP</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\n-   This [chapter](./doc/usp_zephyr_lbm_porting_guide.md) explains how to port existing LoRa Basics Modem application to USP Zephyr.\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>Power Consumption</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\nZephyr RTOS implements a way of handling the power states of the used devices (called \"Power Management\" (PM) actions). Basically, it offers a simple way for the RTOS to \"tell\" connected devices to enter sleep mode when Zephyr does so. However, as it's done without any driver intervention, the timing when the devices enter/exit sleep mode can't be precisely controlled, leading to a possible increase of power consumption. \\\nAs so, Semtech radio drivers **don't** use Zephyr system for handling sleep mode, and are entered sleep as soon as possible to optimize power consumption.\nIt is important to note that the Zephyr PM actions are correctly handled by the internal MCU peripherals, allowing the samples to reach the following current consumption values when in sleep:\n\n| Board | Current (uA) |\n| ----- | ------------ |\n| Xiao-nRF54L15 | ~30<sup>1</sup> |\n| nRF52840-DK | ~505/~25<sup>2</sup> |\n| nRF54L15-DK | ~18.1<sup>3</sup> |\n| NUCLEO-L476RG | ~5 | |\n\nTo reach low power, use `prj_lowpower.conf` when building, disabling logs:\n```bash\nwest build --pristine --board xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_wio_lr2021 usp_zephyr/samples/usp/lbm/periodical_uplink -- -DCONF_FILE=\"prj_lowpower.conf\"\n```\n\nNotes :\n- Be aware of differencies when using `CONFIG_PM_DEVICE_RUNTIME` or `CONFIG_PM_DEVICE_SYSTEM_MANAGED` in your prj.conf file.\n\n> <sup>1</sup> It is impossible to measure only the 3.3V used to power the nRF54L15 on the Xiao-nRF54L15 board, as Seeed didn’t provide for that in the design. Instead, we have to measure the whole current supplied to the board via the VBAT pads. This does include the LR2021 IC, the DC/DC buck converter and a few more active components. For the measurement, the VBAT voltage was 3.7V (Li-Ion nominal voltage).\n\n> <sup>2</sup> Measured @VDD = 3V. Due du a [documented nRF52840 anomaly](https://docs.nordicsemi.com/bundle/errata_nRF52840_Rev3/page/ERR/nRF52840/Rev3/latest/anomaly_840_195.html), this chip draws more current when SPI3 is used, and SPI3 is the default one routed on the board’s Arduino header. Using SPI0 instead of SPI3 will lead to ~25uA.\n\n> <sup>3</sup> Measured @VDD = 3.3V. The nRF54L15 can go down to ~3µA, but as we have to use SPI0 peripheral as [cross power-domain](https://docs.nordicsemi.com/bundle/ps_nrf54L15/page/chapters/pin.html#d380e188), it draws a few more µA.\n\n\n\n</details>\n\n<details>\n    <summary><strong>Troubleshooting</strong></summary>\n<br>\n\nThis section presents frequentely-encountered errors and how to fix them.\n\n| Description | Cause | Workaround |\n| :---------- | :---- | :--------- |\n| Nothing outputs to the serial console when plugged. | <ul><li>The serial port opened isn't the board serial port, or the serial port configuration is wrong.</li><li>The board or the shield isn't properly connected.</li><li>The BUSY pin is held high by the radio.</li></ul> | Open another serial port or change serial port configuration. Check if board/shield is properly plugged and in the right orientation. Try another radio shield. |\n| I can't see LoRa messages on my NS console. | <ul><li>The programmed region is wrong.</li><li>The antenna is disconnected or faulty.</li><li>You are not in range of any LoRa gateway connected to your NS.</li><li>The entered user credentials are wrong.</li></ul> | Check if the programmed region corresponds to your geographic location. Check the antenna connection. Check if you have a gateway in range, or host a gateway. Check the user credentials (devEUI, joinEUI, appKey).\n\nWhen using RAC or LBM API, you can encounter \"Modem Panic Messages\". [This documentation](https://github.com/Lora-net/usp#troubleshooting) is available for more details on how to deal with those issues.\n\n</details>\n"
```json
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

Dự án này là **USP for Zephyr**, một nền tảng phần mềm tích hợp **Unified Software Platform (USP)** của Semtech vào hệ điều hành thời gian thực **Zephyr RTOS**.

Dưới đây là các điểm chính để bạn nắm bắt nhanh dự án:

### 1. Mục tiêu và Công nghệ
*   **Mục tiêu:** Cung cấp giải pháp kết nối không dây tiên tiến sử dụng công nghệ **LoRa® thế hệ thứ 4**.
*   **Giao thức:** Hỗ trợ đa giao thức (multi-protocol) thông qua thư viện USP của Semtech.
*   **Hệ điều hành:** Chạy trên nền **Zephyr RTOS** (phiên bản khuyến nghị v4.2.0), giúp tận dụng tính module hóa và khả năng di động (portability) cực cao của Zephyr.

### 2. Cấu trúc phần cứng (Hardware)
Dựa trên cấu trúc thư mục, dự án hiện đang nhắm tới:
*   **Chip điều khiển (MCU):** Nordic **nRF54L15** (một dòng SoC mới, tiết kiệm năng lượng của Nordic).
*   **Board mạch:** **Seeed Studio XIAO nRF54L15**.
*   **Module Radio (Shield):** **Semtech Wio-LR2021** (sử dụng chip LR2021).
*   **Khả năng mở rộng:** Dự án cũng hỗ trợ các dòng board khác như STM32 (Nucleo-L476RG) và các dòng nRF52 khác.

### 3. Cấu trúc thư mục quan trọng
*   `application/`: Chứa mã nguồn ứng dụng chính, các ví dụ (samples) và cấu hình manifest (`west.yml`). Đây là nơi bạn sẽ làm việc chủ yếu.
*   `zephyr/`: Nhân hệ điều hành Zephyr RTOS.
*   `modules/lib/usp`: Thư viện lõi USP của Semtech (được quản lý như một submodule).
*   `bootloader/mcuboot/`: Trình quản lý khởi động (bootloader) giúp cập nhật firmware an toàn.
*   `.venv/`: Môi trường ảo Python chứa các công cụ cần thiết như `west`, `pyocd` (để nạp chip), `imgtool` (quản lý image).
*   `build/`: Nơi chứa các tệp tin sau khi biên dịch (như tệp `.elf` bạn thấy ở thư mục gốc).

### 4. Cách thức hoạt động
Dự án sử dụng công cụ **West** (công cụ quản lý của Zephyr) để quản lý các kho mã nguồn (repositories) khác nhau.
*   **Biên dịch:** Sử dụng lệnh `west build`.
*   **Nạp chương trình:** Sử dụng `west flash` (thường thông qua công cụ `pyocd` cho dòng nRF54).
*   **Ví dụ:** Các mẫu ứng dụng nằm trong `application/samples/usp/`, bao gồm các tính năng như gửi dữ liệu định kỳ (`periodical_uplink`), đo khoảng cách (`ranging`), v.v.

Bạn có muốn tôi đi sâu vào tệp tin cụ thể nào hoặc hướng dẫn cách biên dịch thử một ví dụ không?

---

and debug output\n\n# Configuration and Build\n\n## Using CMake\n\nMost examples can be configured at compile time by passing `-D` flags to CMake.\nThese flags are documented in a table.\nWhen building using `west`, the syntax is as follow:\n```bash\nwest build --pristine --board <board> --shield <shield> <sample> -- -DEXTRA_CFLAGS=\"<list of additional -D flags>\"\n```\n\nAll examples use the unified logging system, which is controlled with the following flags:\n\n| Parameter                    | Default   | Description                                         |\n|------------------------------|-----------|-----------------------------------------------------|\n| `RAC_LOGGING_ENABLE`         | `ON`      | Enable logging system                               |\n| `RAC_LOG_PROFILE`            | `DEFAULT` | logging profile (MINIMAL;DEFAULT;VERBOSE;DEBUG;ALL) |\n|------------------------------|-----------|-----------------------------------------------------|\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_ERROR_ENABLE`  | `ON`      | Enable RAC Core ERROR logs                          |\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_CONFIG_ENABLE` | `ON`      | Enable RAC Core CONFIG logs                         |\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_INFO_ENABLE`   | `OFF`     | Enable RAC Core INFO logs                           |\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_WARN_ENABLE`   | `OFF`     | Enable RAC Core WARN logs                           |\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_DEBUG_ENABLE`  | `OFF`     | Enable RAC Core DEBUG logs                          |\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_API_ENABLE`    | `OFF`     | Enable RAC Core API logs                            |\n| `RAC_CORE_LOG_RADIO_ENABLE`  | `OFF`     | Enable RAC Core RADIO logs                          |\n|------------------------------|-----------|-----------------------------------------------------|\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_TX_ENABLE`     | `ON`      | Enable RAC LoRa TX logs                             |\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_RX_ENABLE`     | `ON`      | Enable RAC LoRa RX logs                             |\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_CONFIG_ENABLE` | `ON`      | Enable RAC LoRa CONFIG logs                         |\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_ERROR_ENABLE`  | `ON`      | Enable RAC LoRa ERROR logs                          |\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_INFO_ENABLE`   | `OFF`     | Enable RAC LoRa INFO logs                           |\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_WARN_ENABLE`   | `OFF`     | Enable RAC LoRa WARN logs                           |\n| `RAC_LORA_LOG_DEBUG_ENABLE`  | `OFF`     | Enable RAC LoRa DEBUG logs                          |\n\n## Using the Device Tree\n\nSome examples require LoRaWAN Parameters. Configure these parameters in your device tree or overlay file:\n\n```dts\n&{/zephyr,user} {\n    user-lorawan-device-eui = [00 01 02 03 04 05 06 07];\n    user-lorawan-join-eui = [00 01 02 03 04 05 06 07];\n    user-lorawan-gen-app-key = [00 01 02 03 04 05 06 07 08 09 0A 0B 0C 0D 0E 0F];\n    user-lorawan-app-key = [00 01 02 03 04 05 06 07 08 09 0A 0B 0C 0D 0E 0F];\n    user-lorawan-region = \"EU868\";\n};\n```\n\n## Flash and Run\n\n- Flash the firmware to your MCU board equipped with the Semtech&copy radio.\n```\nwest flash # optional --runner parameter may be given\n```\n\n# Common issues\n\n1. **Build/compilation failure**:\n   - Check that radio parameters are properly configured in CMake\n   - Ensure USP environment is correctly set up\n   - Ensure correct shield and board configuration\n\n2. **Communication issues**:\n   - Verify frequency, sync word, and network settings match between devices\n\n3. **No packets received**:\n   - Verify that radio parameters are identical on both devices\n   - Check frequency and proximity of devices\n\n4. **Very high PER**:\n   - Increase transmission power\n   - Reduce distance between devices\n   - Change channel/frequency\n\n5. **Join failures**:\n   - Check LoRaWAN credentials and network server configuration\n\n6. **No ranging results/ranging failure**:\n   - Check device positioning (line of sight recommended)\n   - Verify both devices use same configuration\n   - Ensure adequate distance (minimum ~1 meter)\n\n7. **Timeout errors**:\n   - Check RF environment for interference\n   - Verify antenna connections\n   - Try different frequency or power settings\n\n8. **Inconsistent Results**:\n   - Ensure stable device positioning\n   - Check for RF reflections or multipath\n   - Consider environmental factors (weather, obstacles)\n\n9. **OLED Display Issues**:\n   - Verify I2C connections and address\n   - Check display power supply\n   - Ensure SSD1306 driver configuration\n\n# Debug\n\n## Debugging output\n\nAll applications provide comprehensive debug output via UART.\nUse a terminal emulator like `minicom` to monitor:\n```bash\nminicom -D /dev/ttyACM0 [-b <baudrate>]\n```\nThe default baudrate used is 115200. But check on your MCU applicaiton overlay file (e.g. `samples/usp/lbm/periodical_uplink/boards/xiao_nrf54l15_nrf54l15_cpuapp.overlay`\n\n## Stepping through code\n\n1. Open a GDB server on the chip using OpenOCD or pyOCD\n   ```bash\n   openocd -f interface/stlink.cfg -f target/stm32l4x.cfg [-c \"gdb_port <GDB_PORT>\"]\n   ```\n   The default GDB port is 3333.\n\n2. Open the flashed binary with GDB (preferably with the ELF format)\n   ```bash\n   gdb path/to/binary\n   ```\n\n3. In GDB, connect to the device and restart its execution\n   ```\n   >>> target extended-remote :<GDB_PORT>\n   >>> monitor reset halt\n   ```\n\nYou can now proceed with the usual GDB commands, like `break main` and `continue`.\n"
  }

|\n|------------------------------|---------------|------------------------------------------------|\n| `PERIODICAL_UPLINK_DELAY_S`  | `60`          | Interval between periodic uplinks (seconds) |\n|------------------|---------------------|--------------------------------------|\n| Standard         | `prj.conf`          | Full logging and debug capabilities  |\n| Low Power        | MHz (GRP3)  |\n| `AS_923_GRP4`     | Asia-Pacific 923 MHz (GRP4)  |\n| `AU_915`  | Australia 915 MHz     |\n| `CN_470`  | China 470 MHz (RP2)         |\n| `CN_470_RP_1_0` | China 470 MHz (RP1) |\n| `IN_865`  | India 865 MHz         |\n| `KR_920`     | South Korea 920 MHz |\n| `RU_864`     | Russia 864 MHz  |\n| `WW_2G4`     | WW 2.4GHz  |\n\n## Compilation\n\n### USP Zephyr\n\n**Build standard version:**\n```bash\nwest build --pristine --board xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_loraplus_expansion_board --shield semtech_wio_lr2021 usp_zephyr/samples/usp/lbm/periodical_uplink\n```\n\n**Build low power version:**\n```bash\nwest build --pristine --board xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_loraplus_expansion_board --shield semtech_wio_lr2021 usp_zephyr/samples/usp/lbm/periodical_uplink -- -DCONF_FILE=prj_lowpower.conf\n```\n\n**Flash the firmware:**\n```bash\nwest flash\n```\n\nNote:\n- On STM32L476RG, you can select DMA on SPI by\n  - uncommenting the DMA definition in `nucleo_l476rg.overlay`file,\n  - uncommenting the DMA Kconfig symbols in `prj.conf`\n\n### USP \n**Build sample:**\n```bash\nrm -Rf build/ ; cmake -L -S examples  -B build -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=MinSizeRel -DBOARD=NUCLEO_L476 -DRAC_RADIO=lr2021 -G Ninja; cmake --build build --target periodical_uplink\n```\n\n**Example of `openocd`command to flash:**\n```bash\nopenocd -f interface/stlink.cfg -f target/stm32l4x.cfg -c \"adapter serial <SERIAL_NUMBER>\" -c \"program build/periodical_uplink verify reset exit\"\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n1. **LoRaWAN Network**: Access to a LoRaWAN network (TTN, ChirpStack, etc.)\n2. **Network Credentials**: Valid DevEUI, JoinEUI, and AppKey from your network provider\n3. **Gateway Coverage**: Ensure LoRaWAN gateway coverage in your area\n\n### Setup Steps\n\n1. **Configure Credentials**: Edit `boards/user_keys.overlay` with your LoRaWAN credentials or [USP credentials](../../../../../modules/lib/usp/examples/main_examples/example_options.h)\n2. **Select Region**: Set appropriate region in user_keys.overlay\n3. **Flash Firmware**: Build and flash the application\n4. **Monitor Logs**: Connect serial console to observe join process and uplinks\n\n### Operation\n\n1. **Automatic Join**: Device automatically attempts to join the network on startup\n2. **Periodic Uplinks**: After successful join, sends uplinks on port 101 every 60 seconds\n3. **Button Uplinks**: Press user button to send immediate uplink on port 102\n4. **Downlink Handling**: Receives and logs any downlink messages from network\n\n## Expected Output\n\n### Startup and Join\n```\n[00:00:01.000,000] <inf> usp: LoRaWAN Periodical uplink (60 sec) example is starting\n[00:00:02.100,000] <inf> usp: Event received: RESET\n[00:00:02.200,000] <inf> usp: Event received: JOINED\n[00:00:02.200,000] <inf> usp: Modem is now joined\n```\n\n### Periodic Uplinks\n```\n[00:01:02.300,000] <inf> usp: Event received: ALARM\n[00:01:02.400,000] <inf> usp: Event received: TXDONE\n[00:01:02.400,000] <inf> usp: Transmission done\n[00:02:02.500,000] <inf> usp: Event received: ALARM\n```\n\n### Button-Triggered Uplink\n```\n[00:00:30.200,000] <inf> usp: Button pushed\n[00:00:30.300,000] <inf> usp: Event received: TXDONE\n[00:00:30.300,000] <inf> usp: Transmission done\n```\n\n### Downlink Reception\n```\n[00:01:05.100,000] <inf> usp: Event received: DOWNDATA\n[00:01:05.100,000] <dbg> usp: Data received on port 1\n[00:01:05.100,000] <dbg> usp: Received payload: 48 65 6C 6C 6F\n```\n\n## Technical Notes\n\n- **Uplink Ports**: Periodic uplinks use port 101, button uplinks use port 102\n- **Payload Format**: 4-byte counter (big-endian) incremented with each transmission\n- **Join Method**: OTAA (Over-The-Air Activation) only\n- **Button Debouncing**: 500ms debounce time to prevent multiple triggers\n- **Event-Driven Architecture**: Comprehensive handling of all LBM events\n- **Relay Support**: Optional LoRaWAN relay TX functionality for network extension\n- **Thread Integration**: Full USP thread integration with cooperative scheduling\n\n## Advanced Features\n\n### Relay TX Configuration\nWhen `CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_RELAY_TX=y`:\n- Dynamic relay activation mode\n- Smart level: 8 consecutive uplinks\n- Backoff: 4 WOR frames\n- CSMA protection for WOR transmissions\n\n### Event Handling\n- **Network Events**: JOIN, TXDONE, DOWNDATA, JOINFAIL\n- **Service Events**: FUOTA, multicast, firmware management\n- **Advanced Events**: Relay TX, regional duty cycle, test mode\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n1. **Join Failures**:\n   - Verify credentials in user_keys.overlay or example_options.h\n   - Check LoRaWAN region setting\n   - Ensure gateway coverage\n\n2. **No Uplinks**:\n   - Confirm successful join (JOINED event)\n   - Check duty cycle restrictions\n   - Verify network connectivity\n\n3. **Build Errors**:\n   - Ensure user_keys.overlay or example_options.h are properly configured\n   - Check shield compatibility with board\n   - Verify USP module configuration\n\n### Network Server Configuration\n\n- **Payload Decoder**: 4-byte counter (bytes to uint32, big-endian)\n- **Port Assignment**: Port 101 (periodic), Port 102 (button)\n- **Confirmed Uplinks**: Unconfirmed by default (configurable)\n"
  }
```json
}
```

<zephyr/logging/log.h>\n#include <zephyr/drivers/gpio.h>\n#include <zephyr/lorawan_lbm/lorawan_hal_init.h>\n\n#include <smtc_modem_api.h>\n#include <smtc_modem_test_api.h>\n#include <smtc_modem_utilities.h>\n#include <smtc_modem_hal.h>\n\n#if defined( CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_RELAY_TX )\n#include <smtc_modem_relay_api.h>\n#endif\n\n#include <smtc_zephyr_usp_api.h>\n#include <smtc_sw_platform_helper.h>\n\nLOG_MODULE_REGISTER( usp, LOG_LEVEL_INF );\n\n/**\n * @brief Helper macro that returned a human-friendly message if a command does not return\n * SMTC_MODEM_RC_OK\n *\n * @remark The macro is implemented to be used with functions returning a @ref\n * smtc_modem_return_code_t\n *\n * @param[in] rc  Return code\n */\n\nvoid assert_smtc_modem_rc( const char* file, const char* func, int line, smtc_modem_return_code_t rc )\n{\n    char* rc_msg = \"\";\n    int   level  = -1;\n\n    if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_NOT_INIT )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_NOT_INIT );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_ERR;\n    }\n    else if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_INVALID )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_INVALID );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_ERR;\n    }\n    else if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_BUSY )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_BUSY );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_ERR;\n    }\n    else if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_FAIL )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_FAIL );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_ERR;\n    }\n    else if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_INVALID_STACK_ID )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_INVALID_STACK_ID );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_ERR;\n    }\n    else if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_NO_TIME )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_NO_TIME );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_WRN;\n    }\n    else if( rc == SMTC_MODEM_RC_NO_EVENT )\n    {\n        rc_msg = STRINGIFY( SMTC_MODEM_RC_NO_EVENT );\n        level  = LOG_LEVEL_INF;\n    }\n\n    if( level == LOG_LEVEL_INF )\n    {\n        LOG_INF( \"In %s - %s (line %d): %s\", file, func, line, rc_msg );\n    }\n    else if( level == LOG_LEVEL_WRN )\n    {\n        LOG_WRN( \"In %s - %s (line %d): %s\", file, func, line, rc_msg );\n    }\n    else if( level == LOG_LEVEL_ERR )\n    {\n        LOG_ERR( \"In %s - %s (line %d): %s\", file, func, line, rc_msg );\n    }\n}\n\n#define ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( rc_func ) assert_smtc_modem_rc( __FILE__, __func__, __LINE__, rc_func )\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE CONSTANTS -------------------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/**\n * Stack id value (multistacks modem is not yet available)\n */\n#define STACK_ID 0\n\n/**\n * @brief Stack credentials\n */\n\n#if !defined( CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_CRYPTOGRAPHY_LR11XX_WITH_CREDENTIALS )\nstatic const uint8_t user_dev_eui[8]      = DT_PROP( DT_PATH( zephyr_user ), user_lorawan_device_eui );\nstatic const uint8_t user_join_eui[8]     = DT_PROP( DT_PATH( zephyr_user ), user_lorawan_join_eui );\nstatic const uint8_t user_gen_app_key[16] = DT_PROP( DT_PATH( zephyr_user ), user_lorawan_gen_app_key );\nstatic const uint8_t user_app_key[16]     = DT_PROP( DT_PATH( zephyr_user ), user_lorawan_app_key );\n#endif\n\n#define DT_MODEM_REGION( region ) DT_CAT( SMTC_MODEM_REGION_, region )\n\n#define MODEM_REGION DT_MODEM_REGION( DT_STRING_UNQUOTED( DT_PATH( zephyr_user ), user_lorawan_region ) )\n\n/**\n * @brief Watchdog counter reload value during sleep (The period must be lower than MCU watchdog\n * period (here 32s))\n */\n#define WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS 20000\n\n/**\n * @brief Periodical uplink alarm delay in seconds\n */\n#ifndef PERIODICAL_UPLINK_DELAY_S\n#define PERIODICAL_UPLINK_DELAY_S 60\n#endif\n\n#ifndef DELAY_FIRST_MSG_AFTER_JOIN\n#define DELAY_FIRST_MSG_AFTER_JOIN 60\n#endif\n\n/**\n * @brief User button - Disable if not available on user board\n */\n\n#define LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN DT_NODE_EXISTS( DT_ALIAS( smtc_user_button ) )\n\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\nstatic const struct gpio_dt_spec button = GPIO_DT_SPEC_GET( DT_ALIAS( smtc_user_button ), gpios );\nstatic struct gpio_callback      button_cb_data;\n#endif\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE TYPES -----------------------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE VARIABLES -------------------------------------------------------\n */\nstatic uint8_t                  rx_payload[SMTC_MODEM_MAX_LORAWAN_PAYLOAD_LENGTH] = { 0 }; /* Buffer for rx payload */\nstatic uint8_t                  rx_payload_size = 0;     /* Size of the payload in the rx_payload buffer */\nstatic smtc_modem_dl_metadata_t rx_metadata     = { 0 }; /* Metadata of downlink */\nstatic uint8_t                  rx_remaining    = 0;     /* Remaining downlink payload in modem */\nstatic uint32_t                 uplink_counter  = 0;     /* uplink raising counter */\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\nstatic volatile bool user_button_is_press = false; /* Flag for button status */\n#endif\n\n#if defined( CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_RELAY_TX )\nstatic smtc_modem_relay_tx_config_t relay_config = { 0 };\n#endif\n/**\n * @brief Internal credentials\n */\n#if defined( CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_CRYPTOGRAPHY_LR11XX_WITH_CREDENTIALS )\nstatic uint8_t chip_eui[SMTC_MODEM_EUI_LENGTH] = { 0 };\nstatic uint8_t chip_pin[SMTC_MODEM_PIN_LENGTH] = { 0 };\n#endif\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE FUNCTIONS DECLARATION -------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/**\n * @brief User callback for modem event\n *\n *  This callback is called every time an event ( see smtc_modem_event_t ) appears in the modem.\n *  Several events may have to be read from the modem when this callback is called.\n */\nstatic void modem_event_callback( void );\n\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\n/**\n * @brief User callback for button EXTI\n *\n * @param context Define by the user at the init\n */\nstatic void user_button_callback( const void* context );\n\n/**\n * @brief Configure User Button\n *\n */\nstatic int configure_user_button( void );\n#endif\n\n/**\n * @brief Send the 32bits uplink counter on chosen port\n */\nstatic void send_uplink_counter_on_port( uint8_t port );\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC FUNCTIONS DEFINITION ---------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/* A binary semaphore to notify the main LBM loop */\nK_SEM_DEFINE( periodical_uplink_event_sem, 0, 1 );\n\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\n/* for zephyr compat*/\nvoid button_pressed( const struct device* dev, struct gpio_callback* cb, uint32_t pins )\n{\n    printk( \"%s\", __func__ );\n    user_button_callback( dev );\n}\n#endif\n\n/**\n * @brief Example to send a user payload on an external event\n *\n */\nint main( void )\n{\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\n    if( configure_user_button( ) != 0 )\n    {\n        LOG_ERR( \"Issue when configuring user button, aborting\\n\" );\n        return 1;\n    }\n#endif\n\n    LOG_INF( \"LoRaWAN Periodical uplink (%d sec) example is starting\", PERIODICAL_UPLINK_DELAY_S );\n\n    SMTC_SW_PLATFORM_INIT( );\n    SMTC_SW_PLATFORM_VOID( smtc_rac_init( ) );\n    // Call smtc_modem_init() after smtc_rac_init()\n    SMTC_SW_PLATFORM_VOID( smtc_modem_init( &modem_event_callback ) );\n\n    set_led( SMTC_PF_LED_TX, true );\n    set_led( SMTC_PF_LED_RX, false );\n\n    while( true )\n    {\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\n        if( user_button_is_press == true )\n        {\n            user_button_is_press = false;\n            LOG_DBG( \"Button pressed\" );\n\n            smtc_modem_status_mask_t status_mask = 0;\n\n            smtc_modem_get_status( STACK_ID, &status_mask );\n\n            // Check if the device has already joined a network\n            if( ( status_mask & SMTC_MODEM_STATUS_JOINED ) == SMTC_MODEM_STATUS_JOINED )\n            {\n                // Send the uplink counter on port 102\n                send_uplink_counter_on_port( 102 );\n                smtc_modem_hal_wake_up( );\n            }\n        }\n#endif\n\n#if !defined( CONFIG_USP_MAIN_THREAD )\n        uint32_t sleep_time_ms = smtc_modem_run_engine( );\n        smtc_rac_run_engine( );\n        if( smtc_rac_is_irq_flag_pending( ) )\n        {\n            continue;\n        }\n        // Allows waking up on radio event or push-button press\n        struct k_sem* sems[] = { smtc_modem_hal_get_event_sem( ), &periodical_uplink_event_sem };\n        ( void ) wait_on_sems( sems, 2, K_MSEC( MIN( sleep_time_ms, WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS ) ) );\n#else\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\n        if( user_button_is_press == false )\n        {\n            k_sem_take( &periodical_uplink_event_sem, K_MSEC( WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS ) );\n        }\n#else\n        k_sem_take( &periodical_uplink_event_sem, K_MSEC( WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS ) );\n#endif\n#endif\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE FUNCTIONS DEFINITION --------------------------------------------\n */\n\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\nstatic int configure_user_button( void )\n{\n    int ret = 0;\n    if( !gpio_is_ready_dt( &button ) )\n    {\n        printk( \"Error: button device %s is not ready\\n\", button.port->name );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    ret = gpio_pin_configure_dt( &button, GPIO_INPUT );\n    if( ret != 0 )\n    {\n        printk( \"Error %d: failed to configure %s pin %d\\n\", ret, button.port->name, button.pin );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    ret = gpio_pin_interrupt_configure_dt( &button, GPIO_INT_EDGE_TO_ACTIVE );\n    if( ret != 0 )\n    {\n        printk( \"Error %d: failed to configure interrupt on %s pin %d\\n\", ret, button.port->name, button.pin );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    gpio_init_callback( &button_cb_data, button_pressed, BIT( button.pin ) );\n    gpio_add_callback( button.port, &button_cb_data );\n\n    return 0;\n}\n#endif\n\n//  WARNING : Run in USP/RAC Thread if compiled with threads\nstatic void modem_event_callback( void )\n{\n    LOG_DBG( \"Modem event callback\" );\n\n    smtc_modem_event_t current_event = { 0 };\n    uint8_t            event_pending_count;\n    uint8_t            stack_id = STACK_ID;\n\n    /* Continue to read modem event until all event has been processed */\n    do\n    {\n        /* Read modem event */\n        ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_get_event( &current_event, &event_pending_count ) );\n\n        switch( current_event.event_type )\n        {\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_RESET:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: RESET\" );\n\n#if !defined( CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_CRYPTOGRAPHY_LR11XX_WITH_CREDENTIALS )\n            /* Set user credentials */\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_set_deveui( stack_id, user_dev_eui ) );\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_set_joineui( stack_id, user_join_eui ) );\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_set_appkey( stack_id, user_gen_app_key ) );\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_set_nwkkey( stack_id, user_app_key ) );\n#else\n            /* Get internal credentials */\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_get_chip_eui( stack_id, chip_eui ) );\n            SMTC_HAL_TRACE_ARRAY( \"CHIP_EUI\", chip_eui, SMTC_MODEM_EUI_LENGTH );\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_get_pin( stack_id, chip_pin ) );\n            SMTC_HAL_TRACE_ARRAY( \"CHIP_PIN\", chip_pin, SMTC_MODEM_PIN_LENGTH );\n#endif\n            /* Set user region */\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_set_region( stack_id, MODEM_REGION ) );\n            /* Schedule a Join LoRaWAN network */\n#if defined( CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_RELAY_TX )\n            /* by default when relay mode is activated , CSMA is also activated by\n             * default to at least protect the WOR transmission if you want to disable\n             * the csma please uncomment the next line\n             */\n            /* ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC(smtc_modem_csma_set_state (stack_id,false)); */\n\n            relay_config.second_ch_enable = false;\n\n            /* The RelayModeActivation field indicates how the end-device SHOULD manage\n             * the relay mode.\n             */\n            relay_config.activation = SMTC_MODEM_RELAY_TX_ACTIVATION_MODE_DYNAMIC;\n\n            /* number_of_miss_wor_ack_to_switch_in_nosync_mode  field indicates that the\n             * relay mode SHALL be restart in no sync mode when it does not receive a\n             * WOR ACK frame after number_of_miss_wor_ack_to_switch_in_nosync_mode\n             * consecutive uplinks.\n             */\n            relay_config.number_of_miss_wor_ack_to_switch_in_nosync_mode = 3;\n\n            /* smart_level field indicates that the relay mode SHALL be enabled if\n             * the end-device does not receive a valid downlink after\n             * smart_level consecutive uplinks.\n             */\n            relay_config.smart_level = 8;\n\n            /* The BackOff field indicates how the end-device SHALL behave when it does\n             * not receive a WOR ACK frame. BackOff Description 0 Always send a LoRaWAN\n             * uplink 1..63 Send a LoRaWAN uplink after X WOR frames without a WOR ACK\n             */\n            relay_config.backoff = 4;\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_relay_tx_enable( stack_id, &relay_config ) );\n#endif\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_join_network( stack_id ) );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_ALARM:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: ALARM\" );\n            /* Send periodical uplink on port 101 */\n            send_uplink_counter_on_port( 101 );\n            /* Restart periodical uplink alarm */\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_alarm_start_timer( PERIODICAL_UPLINK_DELAY_S ) );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_JOINED:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: JOINED\" );\n            LOG_INF( \"Modem is now joined \" );\n\n            /* Send first periodical uplink on port 101 */\n            send_uplink_counter_on_port( 101 );\n            /* start periodical uplink alarm */\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_alarm_start_timer( DELAY_FIRST_MSG_AFTER_JOIN ) );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TXDONE:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: TXDONE\" );\n            LOG_INF( \"Transmission done \" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_DOWNDATA:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: DOWNDATA\" );\n            /* Get downlink data */\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC(\n                smtc_modem_get_downlink_data( rx_payload, &rx_payload_size, &rx_metadata, &rx_remaining ) );\n\n            LOG_DBG( \"Data received on port %u\", rx_metadata.fport );\n            LOG_HEXDUMP_DBG( rx_payload, rx_payload_size, \"Received payload\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_JOINFAIL:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: JOINFAIL\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_ALCSYNC_TIME:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: ALCSync service TIME\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_LINK_CHECK:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: LINK_CHECK\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_CLASS_B_PING_SLOT_INFO:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: CLASS_B_PING_SLOT_INFO\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_CLASS_B_STATUS:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: CLASS_B_STATUS\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_LORAWAN_MAC_TIME:\n            LOG_WRN( \"Event received: LORAWAN MAC TIME\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_LORAWAN_FUOTA_DONE:\n        {\n            bool status = current_event.event_data.fuota_status.successful;\n\n            if( status == true )\n            {\n                LOG_INF( \"Event received: FUOTA SUCCESSFUL\" );\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                LOG_WRN( \"Event received: FUOTA FAIL\" );\n            }\n            break;\n        }\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NO_MORE_MULTICAST_SESSION_CLASS_C:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: MULTICAST CLASS_C STOP\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NO_MORE_MULTICAST_SESSION_CLASS_B:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: MULTICAST CLASS_B STOP\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NEW_MULTICAST_SESSION_CLASS_C:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: New MULTICAST CLASS_C \" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NEW_MULTICAST_SESSION_CLASS_B:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: New MULTICAST CLASS_B\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_FIRMWARE_MANAGEMENT:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: FIRMWARE_MANAGEMENT\" );\n            if( current_event.event_data.fmp.status == SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_FMP_REBOOT_IMMEDIATELY )\n            {\n                smtc_modem_hal_reset_mcu( );\n            }\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_STREAM_DONE:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: STREAM_DONE\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_UPLOAD_DONE:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: UPLOAD_DONE\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_DM_SET_CONF:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: DM_SET_CONF\" );\n            break;\n\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_MUTE:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: MUTE\" );\n            break;\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_RELAY_TX_DYNAMIC:\n            /* Relay TX dynamic mode has enable or disable the WOR protocol */\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: RELAY_TX_DYNAMIC\" );\n            break;\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_RELAY_TX_MODE:\n            /* Relay TX activation has been updated */\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: RELAY_TX_MODE\" );\n            break;\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_RELAY_TX_SYNC:\n            /* Relay TX synchronisation has changed */\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: RELAY_TX_SYNC\" );\n            break;\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_RELAY_RX_RUNNING:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: RELAY_RX_RUNNING\\n\" );\n#if defined( ADD_CSMA ) && defined( ADD_RELAY_RX )\n            bool csma_state = false;\n            ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_csma_get_state( STACK_ID, &csma_state ) );\n            if( ( current_event.event_data.relay_rx.status == true ) && ( csma_state == true ) )\n            {\n                // Disable CSMA when Relay Rx Is enabled by network\n                ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_csma_set_state( STACK_ID, false ) );\n            }\n#if defined( ENABLE_CSMA_BY_DEFAULT ) && defined( ADD_RELAY_RX )\n            if( current_event.event_data.relay_rx.status == false )\n            {\n                ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_csma_set_state( STACK_ID, true ) );\n            }\n#endif  // ENABLE_CSMA_BY_DEFAULT\n#endif  // ADD_CSMA\n            break;\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_REGIONAL_DUTY_CYCLE:\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: REGIONAL_DUTY_CYCLE\\n\" );\n            break;\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NO_DOWNLINK_THRESHOLD:\n        {\n            LOG_INF( \"Event received: NO_DOWNLINK_THRESHOLD\\n\" );\n            if( current_event.event_data.no_downlink.status != 0 )\n            {\n                // Leave and re-join network\n                smtc_modem_alarm_clear_timer( );\n                ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_leave_network( STACK_ID ) );\n                ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_join_network( STACK_ID ) );\n                LOG_INF( \"Event received: %s-%s\\n\",\n                         current_event.event_data.no_downlink.status & SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NO_RX_THRESHOLD_ADR_BACKOFF_END\n                             ? \"ADR backoff end-\"\n                             : \"\",\n                         current_event.event_data.no_downlink.status & SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_NO_RX_THRESHOLD_USER_THRESHOLD\n                             ? \"-User threshold reached\"\n                             : \"\" );\n            }\n            else  // Event cleared\n            {\n                LOG_INF( \"Event type: Cleared\\n\" );\n            }\n            break;\n        }\n        case SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE:\n        {\n            uint8_t status_test_mode = current_event.event_data.test_mode_status.status;\n            char*   status_name[]    = { \"SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_ENDED\", \"SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_TX_COMPLETED\",\n                                         \"SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_TX_DONE\", \"SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_RX_DONE\",\n                                         \"SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_RX_ABORTED\" };\n            // When aborted, do not print the status to avoid log flooding\n            if( status_test_mode < SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_RX_ABORTED )\n            {\n                LOG_DBG( \"Event received: TEST_MODE :  %s\\n\", status_name[status_test_mode] );\n            }\n            if( status_test_mode == SMTC_MODEM_EVENT_TEST_MODE_RX_DONE )\n            {\n                int16_t rssi;\n                int16_t snr;\n                uint8_t rx_payload_length;\n                smtc_modem_test_get_last_rx_packets( &rssi, &snr, rx_payload, &rx_payload_length );\n                LOG_HEXDUMP_DBG( rx_payload, rx_payload_length, \"rx_payload\" );\n                LOG_INF( \"rssi: %d, snr: %d\\n\", rssi, snr );\n            }\n            break;\n        }\n\n        default:\n            LOG_ERR( \"Unknown event %u\", current_event.event_type );\n            break;\n        }\n    } while( event_pending_count > 0 );\n}\n\n#if LBM_DTS_HAS_USER_BTN\nstatic void user_button_callback( const void* context )\n{\n    LOG_INF( \"Button pushed\" );\n\n    static uint32_t last_press_timestamp_ms;\n\n    /* Debounce the button press, avoid multiple triggers */\n    if( ( int32_t ) ( smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( ) - last_press_timestamp_ms ) > 500 )\n    {\n        last_press_timestamp_ms = smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( );\n        user_button_is_press    = true;\n    }\n    /* Wake up the main thread */\n    k_sem_give( &periodical_uplink_event_sem );\n}\n#endif\n\nstatic void send_uplink_counter_on_port( uint8_t port )\n{\n    /* Send uplink counter on port 102 */\n    uint8_t buff[4] = { 0 };\n\n    buff[0] = ( uplink_counter >> 24 ) & 0xFF;\n    buff[1] = ( uplink_counter >> 16 ) & 0xFF;\n    buff[2] = ( uplink_counter >> 8 ) & 0xFF;\n    buff[3] = ( uplink_counter & 0xFF );\n    ASSERT_SMTC_MODEM_RC( smtc_modem_request_uplink( STACK_ID, port, false, buff, 4 ) );\n    /* Increment uplink counter */\n    uplink_counter++;\n}\n\n/* --- EOF ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n"
  }
}

## MODEL ✨

**Tool Command**:
```json
{

* @brief Watchdog counter reload value during sleep (The period must be lower than MCU watchdog period (here 32s))\n */\n#define WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS 20000\n\n/**\n * @brief Blue user button or BUTTON 1 on nrf52840-dk\n */\n\n#define USER_BUTTON_NODE DT_ALIAS( smtc_user_button )\n#if !DT_NODE_HAS_STATUS( USER_BUTTON_NODE, okay )\n#error \"Unsupported board: smtc-user-button devicetree alias is not defined\"\n#endif\nstatic const struct gpio_dt_spec button = GPIO_DT_SPEC_GET_OR( USER_BUTTON_NODE, gpios, { 0 } );\nstatic struct gpio_callback      button_cb_data;\n\n/*\n * -------------------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE FUNCTIONS DECLARATION -------------------------------------------\n * Prototypes for internal helper functions.\n */\n\n/**\n * @brief User callback for button EXTI\n *\n * @param context Define by the user at the init\n */\nstatic void user_button_callback( const void* context );\n\n/**\n * @brief Configure User Button\n *\n */\nstatic int configure_user_button( void );\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC FUNCTIONS DEFINITION ---------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/* A binary semaphore to notify the main LBM loop */\nK_SEM_DEFINE( periodical_uplink_event_sem, 0, 1 );\n\n/* for zephyr compat*/\nvoid button_pressed( const struct device* dev, struct gpio_callback* cb, uint32_t pins )\n{\n    printk( \"%s\", __func__ );\n    user_button_callback( dev );\n}\n\nint main( void )\n{\n    if( configure_user_button( ) != 0 )\n    {\n        LOG_ERR( \"Issue when configuring user button, aborting\\n\" );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    SMTC_HAL_TRACE_INFO( \"===== Ping Pong example =====\\r\\n\" );\n\n    SMTC_SW_PLATFORM_INIT( );\n    SMTC_SW_PLATFORM_VOID( smtc_rac_init( ) );\n\n    // initialize LEDs\n    init_leds( );\n    set_led( SMTC_PF_LED_TX, false );\n    set_led( SMTC_PF_LED_RX, false );\n\n    // initialize and start applications\n    ping_pong_init( );\n    periodic_uplink_init( );\n\n    // Main application loop\n    while( true )\n    {\n        // Check button\n        if( user_button_is_press == true )\n        {\n            user_button_is_press = false;\n\n            ping_pong_on_button_press( );\n            periodic_uplink_on_button_press( );\n        }\n\n#if !defined( CONFIG_USP_MAIN_THREAD )\n        smtc_rac_run_engine( );\n        if( smtc_rac_is_irq_flag_pending( ) )\n        {\n            continue;\n        }\n        // Allows waking up on radio event or push-button press\n        struct k_sem* sems[] = { smtc_modem_hal_get_event_sem( ), &periodical_uplink_event_sem };\n        ( void ) wait_on_sems( sems, 2, K_MSEC( WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS ) );\n#else\n        if( user_button_is_press == false )\n        {\n            k_sem_take( &periodical_uplink_event_sem, K_MSEC( WATCHDOG_RELOAD_PERIOD_MS ) );\n        }\n#endif\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE FUNCTIONS DEFINITION --------------------------------------------\n */\n\nstatic int configure_user_button( void )\n{\n    int ret = 0;\n    if( !gpio_is_ready_dt( &button ) )\n    {\n        printk( \"Error: button device %s is not ready\\n\", button.port->name );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    ret = gpio_pin_configure_dt( &button, GPIO_INPUT );\n    if( ret != 0 )\n    {\n        printk( \"Error %d: failed to configure %s pin %d\\n\", ret, button.port->name, button.pin );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    ret = gpio_pin_interrupt_configure_dt( &button, GPIO_INT_EDGE_TO_ACTIVE );\n    if( ret != 0 )\n    {\n        printk( \"Error %d: failed to configure interrupt on %s pin %d\\n\", ret, button.port->name, button.pin );\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    gpio_init_callback( &button_cb_data, button_pressed, BIT( button.pin ) );\n    gpio_add_callback( button.port, &button_cb_data );\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\nstatic void user_button_callback( const void* context )\n{\n    LOG_INF( \"Button pushed\\n\" );\n\n    ( void ) context;  // Not used in the example - avoid warning\n\n    static uint32_t last_press_timestamp_ms = 0;\n\n    // Debounce the button press, avoid multiple triggers\n    if( ( int32_t ) ( smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( ) - last_press_timestamp_ms ) > 500 )\n    {\n        last_press_timestamp_ms = smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( );\n        user_button_is_press    = true;\n    }\n    // Wake up the main thread\n    k_sem_give( &periodical_uplink_event_sem );\n}\n\n/* --- EOF ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n"
  }
```

---

## MODEL ✨

Dựa trên việc phân tích mã nguồn và tài liệu, các mẫu ứng dụng (samples) trong dự án được chia thành 3 nhóm chính, phục vụ các mục đích phát triển khác nhau:

### 1. Nhóm LBM (LoRa Basics Modem)
Đây là nhóm các ứng dụng sử dụng bộ stack LoRaWAN hoàn chỉnh của Semtech.
*   **Mục đích:** Dùng cho các ứng dụng kết nối vào mạng LoRaWAN (như The Things Network, ChirpStack).
*   **Mẫu tiêu biểu - `periodical_uplink`:**
    *   **Cơ chế:** Tự động thực hiện quy trình Join mạng (OTAA) và gửi dữ liệu định kỳ (mặc định mỗi 60 giây).
    *   **Cấu trúc mã nguồn (`main.c`):** 
        *   Sử dụng `smtc_modem_init()` để khởi tạo stack.
        *   Mọi hoạt động được xử lý thông qua một hàm callback sự kiện (`modem_event_callback`). Các sự kiện quan trọng bao gồm: `RESET` (để thiết lập cấu hình vùng/Region và khóa/Keys), `JOINED` (khi đã vào mạng thành công), `TXDONE` (khi gửi xong), và `DOWNDATA` (khi nhận dữ liệu từ server).
    *   **Cấu hình:** Các thông tin quan trọng như DevEUI, AppKey được cấu hình trực tiếp trong tệp Device Tree Overlay (`boards/user_keys.overlay`).

### 2. Nhóm RAC (Radio Abstraction Component)
Đây là lớp trừu tượng hóa phần cứng radio, nằm dưới lớp Modem.
*   **Mục đích:** Dành cho các nhà phát triển muốn điều khiển radio ở mức thấp hơn mà không cần dùng đến stack LoRaWAN, hoặc muốn tự xây dựng giao thức riêng.
*   **Mẫu tiêu biểu - `cad` (Channel Activity Detection):**
    *   Sử dụng radio để dò tìm xem có hoạt động nào trên kênh tần số hay không trước khi truyền (tránh xung đột).
    *   Cho phép can thiệp sâu vào các tham số RF như tần số, băng thông, Spreading Factor (SF).

### 3. Nhóm SDK (Software Development Kit)
Nhóm này chứa các ứng dụng trình diễn các tính năng đặc thù của phần cứng radio Semtech.
*   **Mục đích:** Thử nghiệm hiệu năng và các tính năng nâng cao.
*   **Mẫu tiêu biểu:**
    *   **`ping_pong`:** Kết nối điểm-đối-điểm (P2P) giữa hai thiết bị để kiểm tra khoảng cách và độ ổn định.
    *   **`ranging_demo`:** Tính năng đo khoảng cách giữa hai thiết bị bằng sóng radio (đặc trưng của dòng chip LR11xx).
    *   **`spectral_scan`:** Quét phổ tần số để phân tích nhiễu môi trường.

### Điểm chung trong thiết kế các mẫu:
1.  **Kiến trúc dựa trên sự kiện (Event-driven):** Các ứng dụng không chạy vòng lặp vô tận tiêu tốn CPU mà thường ở trạng thái ngủ (Sleep), chỉ thức dậy khi có sự kiện từ Radio hoặc từ người dùng (nhấn nút).
2.  **Tận dụng Zephyr:** Sử dụng hệ thống logging đồng nhất, quản lý năng lượng (Power Management) và cấu hình phần cứng qua Device Tree.
3.  **Hỗ trợ đa nền tảng:** Cùng một mã nguồn có thể biên dịch cho nhiều loại board khác nhau (nRF54, STM32) bằng cách thay đổi tham số `--board` khi dùng lệnh `west build`.

Bạn có muốn tôi hướng dẫn chi tiết cách cấu hình khóa LoRaWAN để chạy thử mẫu `periodical_uplink` trên board của bạn không?

## MODEL ✨

Việc chuyển mã nguồn từ một dự án mẫu (Workspace lớn) sang một dự án riêng (Custom Project) là cách làm rất đúng để giữ cho code của bạn gọn gàng và dễ quản lý phiên bản (Git).

Trong hệ sinh thái Zephyr, cách sạch sẽ nhất cho bạn lúc này là biến dự án `lr2021-tdoa-firmware` thành một **"Freestanding Application"**. Dự án của bạn sẽ chỉ chứa code logic, còn bộ khung Zephyr và thư viện Semtech USP sẽ được trỏ tới thư mục cũ.

Dưới đây là các bước để bạn chuyển mẫu `periodical_uplink` (mẫu cơ bản nhất) sang dự án mới:

### Bước 1: Copy cấu trúc mã nguồn
Bạn hãy chạy các lệnh sau (hoặc thực hiện qua trình quản lý file) để đưa các file cần thiết sang:

1.  **Copy code chính:**
    Copy file `main.c` từ mẫu vào thư mục `src` của bạn.
2.  **Copy cấu hình:**
    Copy file `prj.conf` (cấu hình tính năng) và thư mục `boards/` (cấu hình phần cứng/phím bấm) từ mẫu sang.

### Bước 2: Tạo file `CMakeLists.txt` cho dự án mới
Tại thư mục gốc của `/home/dashtrad/Documents/lr2021-tdoa-firmware`, bạn tạo một file tên là `CMakeLists.txt` với nội dung sau:

```cmake
cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.20)

# Trỏ tới thư mục chứa Zephyr và module USP
# (Bạn có thể sửa đường dẫn này nếu sau này di chuyển thư mục workspace)
set(ZEPHYR_BASE /home/dashtrad/lora_usp_workspace/zephyr)
find_package(Zephyr REQUIRED HINTS $ENV{ZEPHYR_BASE})

project(lr2021-tdoa-firmware)

# Thêm mã nguồn của bạn
target_sources(app PRIVATE src/main.c)
```

### Bước 3: Cấu hình môi trường biên dịch
Để dự án mới nhận diện được thư viện **USP**, bạn cần cho Zephyr biết module đó nằm ở đâu. Bạn tạo thêm một file tên là `zephyr_modules.txt` hoặc đơn giản là khai báo khi biên dịch.

Tuy nhiên, cách đơn giản nhất để không phải cấu hình loằng ngoằng là tận dụng file cấu hình `west` hiện có.

### Đề xuất cấu trúc file cuối cùng cho dự án của bạn:
Dự án của bạn sẽ trông như thế này (rất sạch sẽ):
```text
lr2021-tdoa-firmware/
├── boards/               # Copy từ mẫu qua (chứa file .overlay và .conf cho từng loại board)
├── src/
│   └── main.c            # Code chính của bạn
├── CMakeLists.txt        # File vừa tạo ở Bước 2
├── prj.conf              # Copy từ mẫu qua
└── .gitignore
```

### Bước 4: Cách biên dịch dự án mới
Bây giờ, thay vì chạy lệnh trong thư mục cũ, bạn mở terminal tại dự án mới và chạy:

```bash
# Kích hoạt môi trường ảo cũ (vì nó chứa các tool cần thiết như west, nrfutil...)
source /home/dashtrad/lora_usp_workspace/.venv/bin/activate

# Biên dịch dự án mới, trỏ module sang thư mục cũ
west build -b xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp -- -DZEPHYR_MODULES=/home/dashtrad/lora_usp_workspace/application
```

**Lợi ích của cách này:**
*   Dự án của bạn chỉ nặng vài KB, dễ dàng push lên Github riêng.
*   Bạn vẫn dùng chung được bộ SDK và Thư viện của hãng mà không cần copy hàng GB dữ liệu qua lại.
*   Mọi thay đổi trong `main.c` của bạn không làm ảnh hưởng đến dự án gốc của hãng.

Bạn có muốn tôi giúp thực hiện việc copy và tạo file `CMakeLists.txt` này ngay bây giờ không?

## MODEL ✨

Chúc mừng bạn, bộ kit **LR2021EVK1XxS1** bạn đang có là dòng mới nhất (tháng 10/2025) sử dụng chip **LR2021** (hỗ trợ cả Sub-GHz và 2.4GHz) kết hợp với MCU **nRF54L15** cực kỳ mạnh mẽ và tiết kiệm điện.

Để chuyển đổi các mẫu sang dự án `lr2021-tdoa-firmware` của bạn một cách chuyên nghiệp và gọn gàng, tôi sẽ thực hiện các bước sau ngay bây giờ:

1.  **Thiết lập cấu trúc thư mục** chuẩn Zephyr trong dự án mới.
2.  **Tạo file `CMakeLists.txt`** và **`prj.conf`** được tối ưu cho bộ kit của bạn.
3.  **Copy mẫu `periodical_uplink`** sang làm "xương sống" để bạn phát triển tính năng TDOA.
4.  **Thiết lập các file Overlay** để định nghĩa đúng các chân kết nối giữa XIAO nRF54L15 và Expansion Board V2a.

## MODEL ✨

Tôi đã thiết lập xong bộ khung dự án cho bạn tại `/home/dashtrad/Documents/lr2021-tdoa-firmware`. Bây giờ dự án của bạn đã rất gọn gàng và sẵn sàng để phát triển tính năng TDOA.

### 1. Cấu trúc dự án mới của bạn:
*   `src/main.c`: Mã nguồn chính (đã copy từ mẫu `periodical_uplink`).
*   `boards/`: Chứa các file cấu hình chân cắm cho board XIAO nRF54L15.
*   `CMakeLists.txt`: Đã được cấu hình để tự động nhận diện thư viện Semtech USP từ thư mục gốc mà không cần copy cả thư viện qua.
*   `prj.conf`: Tệp cấu hình các tính năng của Zephyr (như LoRaWAN, Logging, GPIO).

### 2. Cách biên dịch cho bộ kit LR2021EVK của bạn:
Vì bạn dùng **XIAO nRF54L15** kết hợp với **Expansion Board V2a**, bạn cần dùng lệnh biên dịch với 2 "shield" để Zephyr hiểu đúng sơ đồ nối dây:

```bash
# Di chuyển vào thư mục dự án của bạn
cd /home/dashtrad/Documents/lr2021-tdoa-firmware

# Kích hoạt môi trường ảo (chứa tool biên dịch)
source /home/dashtrad/lora_usp_workspace/.venv/bin/activate

# Biên dịch
west build -b xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_loraplus_expansion_board --shield semtech_wio_lr2021
```

### 3. Cách nạp chương trình:
Sau khi biên dịch xong, bạn chỉ cần cắm board vào và chạy:
```bash
west flash
```
*(Lệnh này sẽ tự động dùng `pyocd` để nạp vào chip nRF54L15 của bạn)*.

### Tiếp theo bạn nên làm gì?
Dự án TDOA thường yêu cầu đo thời gian chính xác và cấu hình Radio ở mức sâu. Bạn có muốn tôi hỗ trợ:
1.  **Chỉnh sửa `main.c`** để chuyển từ gửi dữ liệu định kỳ sang chế độ đo khoảng cách (Ranging/TDOA)?
2.  **Cấu hình vùng tần số** (EU868 hoặc US915) trong file `boards/user_keys.overlay` để khớp với loại anten grey/yellow bạn đang có?

## MODEL ✨

Tôi đã chuyển mã nguồn của mẫu **Ping Pong** sang dự án của bạn và cấu hình lại file `CMakeLists.txt` để nó có thể tự tìm thấy các file logic của Semtech trong thư mục gốc.

Bây giờ bạn có thể tiến hành biên dịch và nạp chương trình. Lưu ý rằng Ping Pong cần **2 thiết bị** chạy cùng code này (một con sẽ là Master, con kia là Slave sau khi nhấn nút) để bắt đầu trao đổi dữ liệu.

### 1. Lệnh biên dịch:
Mở terminal tại thư mục dự án của bạn và chạy:

```bash
# Kích hoạt môi trường (nếu chưa làm)
source /home/dashtrad/lora_usp_workspace/.venv/bin/activate

# Xóa build cũ để đảm bảo sạch sẽ
rm -rf build/

# Biên dịch cho bộ kit nRF54 + LR2021
west build -b xiao_nrf54l15/nrf54l15/cpuapp --shield semtech_loraplus_expansion_board --shield semtech_wio_lr2021
```

### 2. Lệnh nạp:
Cắm thiết bị vào và chạy:
```bash
west flash
```

### 3. Cách kiểm tra:
1.  Nạp code này cho cả 2 bộ thiết bị của bạn.
2.  Mở Serial Terminal (ví dụ: `minicom` hoặc Serial Monitor trong VS Code) với baudrate **115200**.
3.  Bạn sẽ thấy dòng chữ: `===== Ping Pong example =====`.
4.  **Nhấn nút trên một board** để bắt đầu quá trình Ping Pong. 
    *   Board nhấn nút sẽ gửi gói tin "Ping".
    *   Board kia nhận được sẽ tự động phản hồi lại "Pong".
    *   Đèn LED trên board sẽ nhấp nháy mỗi khi truyền/nhận thành công.

Nếu bạn gặp bất kỳ lỗi biên dịch nào (ví dụ: thiếu file header), hãy báo cho tôi biết để tôi điều chỉnh đường dẫn trong `CMakeLists.txt` ngay! Bạn đã sẵn sàng nạp thử chưa?
